,(0x3000, 0x3040)
: 'CJK Symbols and Punctuation'
,(0x3200, 0x3300)
: 'Enclosed CJK Letters and Months'
,(0xfe30, 0xfe50)
: 'CJK Compatibility Forms'
,(0xfe50, 0xfe70)
: 'Small Form Variants'
,(0xff00, 0xfff0)
: 'Halfwidth and Fullwidth Forms'
===

for j in range(0x3000, 0x3040):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0x3200, 0x3300):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xfe30, 0xfe50):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xfe50, 0xfe70):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xff00, 0xfff0):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

def show__j2w__F_W_(ofile, __j2w, /):
  for w_ in 'FW':
    for (i,j), w in __j2w.iter_rng_value_pairs_(reverse=False):
      if not w == w_:continue
      for k in range(i,j):
          ch = chr(k)
          nm = U.name(ch)
          gc = U.category(ch)
          print(f'{w}.{gc}@0x{k:X}:{ch}:{nm}', file=ofile)


show__j2w__F_W_(None, __j2w)

with open(r'/sdcard/0my_files/tmp/å…¨è§’æ ‡ç‚¹-åªä¿ç•™SP-åªä¿ç•™FW.txt', 'xt', encoding='utf8') as ofile:
    show__j2w__F_W_(ofile, __j2w)
